             9.1.36      STE (44h): Set Tear Scanline
       44H                                                                 STE (Set Tear ScanLine )

    Inst / Para        D/CX      WRX        RDX        D8            D7       D6      D5       D4      D3    D2         D1          D0       HEX

       STE               0          ↑         1         -             0        1       0           0   0      1         0           0       (44h)

  1st parameter          1          ↑         1         -            N15     N14      N13      N12     N11   N10        N9          N8

  2nd parameter          1          ↑         1         -            N7       N6      N5       N4      N3    N2         N1          N0

                      -This command turns on the display module’s Tearing Effect output signal on the TE signal line when the display

                      module reaches line N. The TE signal is not affected by changing MV.

                      -The tearing effect line on has one parameter that describes the tearing effect output line mode.

                      -The tearing effect output line consist of V-blanking information only.

       Description                                                                          Tvdl                             Tvdh

                      Vertical time scale


                      Note that set tear scanline with N=0 is equivalent to tearing effect line on with TEM=0.

                      The tearing effect output line shall be active low when the display module is in sleep mode

                      This command takes affect on the frame following the current frame. Therefore, if the tear effect (TE) output is already

    Restriction       on, the TE output shall continue to operate as programmed by the previous tearing effect line on or set tear scanline

                      command until the end of the frame

             9.1.40 WRCTRLD (53h): Write CTRL Display
       53H                                                            WRCTRLD (Write CTRL Display )

    Inst / Para      D/CX       WRX        RDX        D8         D7          D6         D5   D4   D3       D2        D1      D0       HEX

   WRCTRLD             0         ↑           1         -            0        1          0    1        0     0            1   1       (53h)

    Parameter          1          ↑          1         -            0        0     BCTRL     0    DD       BL            0   0

                   -This command is used to control display brightness.

                   -BCTRL: Brightness Control Block On/Off, This bit is always used to switch brightness for display.

                    0 = Off (Brightness register are 00h, DBV[7:0])

                    1 = On (Brightness register are active, according to the other parameters.)



                   -DD: Display Dimming (Only for manual brightness setting)

                    DD = 0: Display Dimming is off.

                    DD = 1: Display Dimming is on.
   Description


                   -BL: Backlight Control On/Off

                    0 = Off (Completely turn off backlight circuit. Control lines must be low.)

                    1 = On



                   -Dimming function is adapted to the brightness registers for display when bit BCTRL is changed at DD=1.

                   -When BL bit changed from ‘on’ to ‘off’, backlight is turned off without gradual dimming, even if dimming-on (DD=1) are

                   selected.

    Restriction

                                      Normal Mode On, Idle Mode Off, Sleep Out                               Yes

              9.1.47 MEMCOMWR (6Ch): Memory Compression Write
     6CH                                                  MEMCOMWR (Memory Compression Write)

  Inst / Para    D/CX WRX RDX             D8      D7         D6          D5         D4      D3        D2             D1        D0    HEX

MEMCOMWR           0      ↑        1       -       0         1            1          0       1         1             0         0     (6Ch)

 1st parameter     1      ↑        1       -    MCW7       MCW6        MCW5        MCW4    MCW3     MCW2            MCW1      MCW0

2nd parameter      1      ↑        1       -   MCW15      MCW14       MCW13        MCW12   MCW11    MCW10           MCW9      MCW8

 3rd parameter     1      ↑        1       -   MCW23      MCW22       MCW21        MCW20   MCW19    MCW18       MCW17      MCW16

 4th parameter     1      ↑        1       -   MCW31      MCW30       MCW29        MCW28   MCW27    MCW26       MCW25      MCW24

                 For 262K Color Format: (when COMFMT=1 in command 6Fh)

                 MCW[7:2]: 6-bit Red subpixel data setting

                 MCW[15:10]: 6-bit Green subpixel data setting

                 MCW[23:18]: 6-bit Blue subpixel data setting

                 MCW[31:24]: Pixel number N=MCW[31:24]+1. (N=1~256)

                 Trigger IC to fill N pixels (the pixel data is depend on MCW[23:2] setting) to RAM when MCW[31:24] is set.


  Description
                 For 65K Color Format: (when COMFMT=0 in command 6Fh)

                 MCW[7:3]: 5-bit Red subpixel data setting

                 MCW[2:0] + MCW[15:13]: 6-bit Green subpixel data setting

                 MCW[12:8]: 5-bit Blue subpixel data setting

                 MCW[23:16]: Pixel number N=MCW[23:16]+1. (N=1~256)

                 Trigger IC to fill N pixels (the pixel data is depend on MCW[15:0] setting) to RAM when MCW[23:16] is set.

                 MCW[31:24]: No function.



                                                        Status                                       Availability

                                       Normal Mode On, Idle Mode Off, Sleep Out                         Yes
   Register

  Availability

              9.1.48 MEMCOMWRC (6Dh): Memory Compression Write Continue
     6DH                                               MEMCOMWRC (Memory Compression Write Continue)

  Inst / Para    D/CX WRX RDX             D8      D7         D6          D5          D4     D3        D2            D1       D0      HEX

MEMCOMWRC          0      ↑       1        -      0           1           1          0       1         1            0         1      (6Dh)

 1st parameter     1      ↑       1        -    MCW7       MCW6        MCW5        MCW4    MCW3     MCW2         MCW1      MCW0

 2nd parameter     1      ↑       1        -   MCW15       MCW14       MCW13       MCW12   MCW11    MCW10        MCW9      MCW8

 3rd parameter     1      ↑       1        -   MCW23       MCW22       MCW21       MCW20   MCW19    MCW18        MCW17    MCW16

 4th parameter     1      ↑       1        -   MCW31       MCW30       MCW29       MCW28   MCW27    MCW26        MCW25    MCW24

                 For 262K color format: (when COMFMT=1 in command 6Fh)

                 MCW[7:2]: 6-bit Red subpixel data setting

                 MCW[15:10]: 6-bit Green subpixel data setting

                 MCW[23:18]: 6-bit Blue subpixel data setting

                 MCW[31:24]: Pixel number (N=MCW[31:24]+1) for write RAM. (N=1~256)

                 Trigger IC to fill N pixels to RAM when MCW[31:24] is set.


  Description
                 For 65K color format: (when COMFMT=0 in command 6Fh)

                 MCW[7:3]: 5-bit Red subpixel data setting

                 MCW[2:0] + MCW[15:13]: 6-bit Green subpixel data setting

                 MCW[12:8]: 5-bit Blue subpixel data setting

                 MCW[23:16]: Pixel number (N=MCW[23:16]+1) for write RAM. (N=1~256)

                 Trigger IC to fill N pixels to RAM when MCW[23:16] is set.

                 MCW[31:24]: No function.

            9.1.49 MEMCOMWREN (6Fh): Memory Compression Write Enable
      6FH                                               MEMCOMWREN (Memory Compression Write Enable)

   Inst / Para    D/CX WRX RDX D8                  D7         D6            D5         D4    D3        D2            D1      D0      HEX

                  COMEN:

                  “0”: disable Memory Compression Write function.

                  “1”: enable Memory Compression Write function.
   Description

            9.2.1       RAMCTRL (B0h): RAM Control
     B0H                                                                        RAMCTR (RAM Control)

  Inst / Para   D/CX     WRX         RDX         D8               D7           D6        D5      D4         D3        D2           D1               D0        HEX

  RAMCTRL           0      ↑          1             -              1           0             1    1          0         0           0                0         (B0h)

1st Parameter       1      ↑          1             -              0           0             0   RM          0         0          DM1           DM0

2nd Parameter       1      ↑          1             -              1           1        EPF1     EPF0      ENDIAN      1          MDT1         MDT0

                RM : ram access selection.
                RM=”0” : Ram access from MCU interface
                RM=”1” : Ram access from RGB interface


                DM[1:0] : Display SYNC operation selection.
                 DM[1:0]                  Mode

                 00h                      Internal clock SYNC mode

                 01h                      RGB interface DOTCLK SYNC mode

                 10h                      VSYNC interface mode

                 11h                      Reserved



                ENDIAN :
                 ENDIAN                   Mode

                 0                        Normal (MSB first)

                 1                        Little Endian (LSB first)
 Description

                Note: Little Endian only can be supported in 65K 8-bit and 9-bit interface.



                                                        1st data input                                                2nd data input

                  Input Data   DB7 DB6 DB5 DB4 DB3 DB2 DB1 DB0                                        DB7 DB6 DB5 DB4 DB3 DB2 DB1 DB0




                          R4    R3        R2   R1          R0             G5       G4   G3            G2    G1   G0          B4        B3      B2        B1    B0




                MDT[1:0] : Method of pixel data transfer.
                Please refer to section 8.8 Data Color Coding

               RIM=”0”: Reserved
               RIM=”1”: 6 bit bus width

            9.2.2       RGBCTRL (B1h): RGB Interface Control
      B1H                                                    RGBCTRL (RGB Interface Control)

   Inst / Para      D/CX    WRX     RDX       D8        D7        D6          D5     D4       D3        D2       D1        D0       HEX

   RGBCTRL              0     ↑       1        -         1          0         1       1        0         0        0         1       (B1h)

  1st parameter         1     ↑       1        -       WO       RCM1      RCM0        0      VSPL     HSPL      DPL        EPL

 2nd parameter          1     ↑       1        -         0       VBP6     VBP5     VBP4      VBP3     VBP2      VBP1      VBP0

  3rd parameter         1     ↑       1        -         0          0         0    HBP4      HBP3     HBP2      HBP1      HBP0

                  WO: Direct RGB mode.
                    WO                                       Mode

                    0                                        Memory

                    1                                        Shift register



                  RCM[1:0]: RGB I/F enable mode selection.
                    RCM[1:0]                                 Mode

                    00
                                                             MCU interface
                    01

                    10                                       RGB DE mode

                    11                                       RGB HV mode



                  VSPL : Sets the signal polarity of the VSYNC pin.
                  VSPL=”0”, Low active
   Description    VSPL=”1”, High active
                  HSPL : Sets the signal polarity of the HSYNC pin.
                  HSPL=”0”, Low active
                  HSPL=”1”, High active
                  DPL : Sets the signal polarity of the DOTCLK pin.
                  DPL = “0” The data is input on the positive edge of DOTCLK
                  DPL = “1” The data is input on the negative edge of DOTCLK
                  EPL : Sets the signal polarity of the ENABLE pin.
                  EPL = “0” The data DB17-0 is written when ENABLE = “1”. Disable data write operation when
                  ENABLE = “0”.
                  EPL = “1” The data DB17-0 is written when ENABLE = “0”. Disable data write operation when
                  ENABLE = “1”.
                  VBP[6:0]: RGB interface Vsync back porch setting. Minimum setting is 0x02.
                  HBP[4:0]: RGB interface Hsync back porch setting. Please refer to the section 8.9.3 for
                  minimum setting.
    Register
   Availability

   Inst / Para      D/CX    WRX       RDX      D8        D7        D6        D5        D4      D3       D2           D1    D0       HEX

                    0                                          Disable separate porch control
   Description

                  BPC[3:0]: Back porch setting in partial mode. The minimum setting is 0x01.
                  FPC[3:0]: Front porch setting in partial mode. The minimum setting is 0x01.

            9.2.4        FRCTRL1 (B3h): Frame Rate Control 1 (In partial mode/ idle colors)
      B3H                                                    FRCTRL1 (Frame rate control 1)

   Inst / Para    D/CX      WRX   RDX      D8       D7       D6        D5        D4         D3        D2         D1          D0      HEX

                 FRSEN: Enable separate frame rate control.
                 When FRSEN=0, Frame rate of idle and partial mode are determined by C6h
                 When FRSEN=1, Frame rate of idle and partial mode are determined by B3h
                    FRSEN                                  Mode

                    0                                      Disable separate FR control

                    1                                      Enable separate FR control

                    DIV[1:0]                               Mode

  Description    NLB[2:0]: Inversion selection in idle mode.

     B6H                                                    PWRSAVCTRL (Power Saving Control)

  Inst / Para     D/CX     WRX    RDX        D8       D7         D6       D5       D4       D3           D2           D1     D0      HEX

PWRSAVCTRL            0      ↑        1       -       1           0        1       1         0           1            1       0      (B6h)

  Parameter           1      ↑        1       -       0           0        0       0         0           0         DSLPINMD DSTBMD

                 DSTBMD:
                 “0”: No Function.
                 “1”: Deep Standby mode.


                 DSLPINMD:
  Description    “0”: Sleep In mode.
                 “1”: Deep Sleep In mode.


                 Note1: It will be necessary to stay at sleep in mode before enter deep sleep in mode.

                 Note2: It will be necessary to wait 10msec after set DSLPINMD=0 to leave deep sleep in mode before sending the other

                 commands.

            9.2.12 FILLRAM (BEh): Fill RAM Function
     BEH                                                         FILLRAM (Fill RAM Function)

  Inst / Para    D/CX   WRX RDX          D8       D7            D6        D5       D4          D3      D2           D1     D0        HEX

   FILLRAM         0      ↑       1       -        1             0         1        1          0       1            1       1       (BEh)

 1st Parameter     1      ↑       1       -        0             0         0        0          0       0            0    FILLEN

2nd Parameter      1      ↑       1       -                            FILLRAM_R[5:0]                               0       0

 3rd Parameter     1      ↑       1       -                            FILLRAM_G[5:0]                               0       0

 4th Parameter     1      ↑       1       -                            FILLRAM_B[5:0]                               0       0

 5th Parameter     1      ↑       1       -    SYNCEN SYNCEDGE           INVX     INVY         0       0            0       0

                 FILLEN:
                 “0”: No Function.
                 “1”: Trigger IC to fill all pixels data in RAM.


                 FILLRAM_R[5:0]: Red subpixel data setting
                 FILLRAM_G[5:0]: Green subpixel data setting
                 FILLRAM_B[5:0]: Blue subpixel data setting


                 SYNCEN: Internal TE signal sync mode enable
                 “0”: Start to fill all pixels data in RAM without wait internal TE signal.
                 “1”: Start to fill all pixels data in RAM when internal TE signal happened.
  Description

                 SYNCEDGE: Internal TE signal edge selection. (when SYNCEN=1)
                 “0”: Leading edge
                 “1”: Ending edge


                 INVX: RAM address counter inversion for X-Direction.
                 “0”: No inversion
                 “1”: Inversion (XOR by MX in command 36h)


                 INVY: RAM address counter inversion for Y-Direction.
                 “0”: No inversion
                 “1”: Inversion (XOR by MY in command 36h)

   Register

  Availability

                                  Partial Mode On, Idle Mode Off, Sleep Out                             Yes

  Description

                  XGS: XOR GS setting in command E4h.

     C7H                                                            CABCCTRL (CABC Control)

  Inst / Para    D/CX    WRX     RDX       D8      D7          D6        D5      D4       D3           D2           D1      D0       HEX

 CABCCTRL          0       ↑        1       -       1          1          0      0         0            1           1        1      (C7h)

 1st Parameter     1       ↑        1       -       0          0          0      0    LEDONREV DPOFPWM PWMFIX PWMPOL

                 LEDONREV: Reverse the status of LED_ON:
                 “0”: keep the status of LED_ON.
                 “1”: reverse the status of LED_ON.
                 DPOFPWM: initial state control of LEDPWM.
                 “0”: The initial state of LEDPWM is low.
                 “1”: The initial state of LEDPWM is high.
  Description
                 PWMFIX: LEDPWM fix control.
                 “0”: LEDPWM control by CABC.
                 “1”: fix LEDPWM in “ON” status.
                 PWMPOL: LEDPWM polarity control.
                 “0”: polarity high.
                 “1”: polarity low.

            9.2.32 GATECTRL (E4h): Gate Control
     E4H                                                           GATECTRL (Gate Control)

  Inst / Para    D/CX    WRX     RDX      D8       D7         D6          D5       D4         D3       D2            D1     D0       HEX

  GATECTRL         0        ↑      1       -        1          1          1         0          0        1            0       0      (E4h)

 1st Parameter     1        ↑      1       -        0          0         NL5      NL4         NL3      NL2          NL1     NL0

 2nd Parameter     1        ↑      1       -        0          0        SCN5     SCN4        SCN3     SCN2          SCN1   SCN0

 3rd Parameter     1        ↑      1       -    S160MD         0          0       TMG          0       SM            0      GS

                 NL[5:0]: Set the number of gate line.
                  NL[5:0]                                                      The number of gate line

                  0x00                                                         8 gate line

                  0x01                                                         16 gate line

                  0x02                                                         24 gate line
                   …




                                                                                …
                  0x27                                                         320 gate line

                 SCN[5:0]: set the first scan line
                  SCN[5:0]                                                     The first scan line

                  0x00                                                         Gate 0

                  0x01                                                         Gate 8
                   …




                                                                                …




                  0x27                                                         Gate 312
  Description

                 S160MD: Source Output mode selection
                 S160MD=”0”: Source output 240 RGB Channel (S1~S720)
                 S160MD=”1”: Source output 160 RGB Channel (S121~S600)


                 TMG: Gate scan mirror mode selection
                 “TMG=0”: when GS=1, gate scan will local mirror (mirror by gate line setting).
                 “TMG=1”: when GS=1, gate scan will full mirror (mirror by 320 gate lines).
                 SM: Gate interlace mode selection
                 SM=”0”: Gate scan using interlace mode.
                 SM=”1”: Gate scan using non-interlace mode.
                 GS: Gate scan direction
                 GS=”0”: Gate scan direction is 0319
                 GS=”1”: Gate scan direction is 3190


   Register
                                                    Status                                           Availability
  Availability
                                  Normal Mode On, Idle Mode Off, Sleep Out                              Yes

                 SPI2EN: 2 data lane enable control.
                 “0”: disable 2 data lane mode.
                 “1”: enable 2 data lane mode

  Description    “0”: commands in command table 2 cannot be read in serial interface
                 “1”: commands in command table 2 can be read in serial interface.


                 Note:

                 It needs one dummy clock if commands in command table 2 need to be read in serial interface.

  Description    In 6bit RGB interface:

                 In 6bit RGB interface:
